<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">On&#160;August 13, 2024,&#160; ParkerVision, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which reported financial and operating results for the six months ended June 30, 2024. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">The information contained in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 hereto, has been &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to liability under that section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing or document.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits.</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#160;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">(d) Exhibits:</div>

<div style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;">&#160;</div>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; width: 100%;">

<body style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; padding: 0in 0.1in; cursor: auto;">
<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: right; font-size: 11pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt;"><b>&nbsp;Exhibit 99.1</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>ParkerVision Reports Second Quarter 2024 Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>JACKSONVILLE</b><b>, Fla.,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="21x1" data-tblname="456618" data-tblv="5" id="led456618F2024431714778551558">August 13, 2024</a>&nbsp;</b>&#8211;<b> </b>ParkerVision, Inc. (OTCQB: PRKR) (&#8220;ParkerVision&#8221; or the "Company"), a developer and marketer of technologies and products for wireless applications, today announced results for the <a data-tblloc="13x1" data-tblname="456618" data-tblv="5" id="led456618F2024431714778571159">six months ended June 30, 2024</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="456618" data-tblv="5" id="led456618F2024431714778584428">2024</a>&nbsp;Summary and Recent Developments</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 18pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">&#9679;
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">The Company is awaiting a decision from the United States Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit (CAFC) in ParkerVision v. Qualcomm (Middle District of Florida - Orlando).</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">In July 2024, the CAFC dismissed the appeal, with the ability for reinstatement, determining that it did not have jurisdiction over this case as the district court had never entered a final order on Qualcomm's counterclaims of invalidity.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">On August 1, 2024, at the joint request of the parties, the District Court in the Middle District of Florida dismissed Qualcomm's counterclaims of invalidity without prejudice, thus providing the CAFC jurisdiction.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">The appeal was resubmitted to the CAFC on August 7, 2024. The CAFC has indicated it will rule on the basis of the briefs previously submitted and the oral arguments heard in November 2023.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 18pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">In June 2024, the Company had a joint claim construction hearing in the Western District of Texas that covered claim construction for pending cases against Texas Instruments ("TI") and NXP Semiconductors ("NXP") and second actions against MediaTek and Realtek. The court's formal claim construction orders are expected to be issued in the near term.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 18pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">The Company has a number of jury trials scheduled in the Western District of Texas beginning in March 2025 against Realtek, followed by April 2025 against MediaTek, May 2025 against TI and August 2025 against NXP.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">MediaTek, TI and NXP have filed inter partes review ("IPR") petitions against claims related to an aggregate of five of the Company's asserted patents. One such IPR has been instituted to date, against one of the patents asserted against MediaTek. The remaining IPRs are still being briefed.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Jeffrey Parker, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#8220;We anticipate that a ruling will be forthcoming from the CAFC in the near term now that the issue of jurisdiction has been resolved.&nbsp; The next twelve months promise to be active as we have four scheduled jury trials in our patent infringement cases in the Western District of Texas.&nbsp; We will also be vigorously defending our patents at the PTAB which has become a commonly used defense strategy for companies attempting to avoid patent infringement judgements."</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Financial Results</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision reported a net loss for the second quarter of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="456618" data-tblv="5" id="led456618F2024431714778477701">2024</a> of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="5" id="led456620F2024431714778493772">$0.3</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="5" id="led456620F2024431714778504659">$0.00</a> per common share, compared to&nbsp;net income of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x2" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="5" id="led456620F2024431714778516608">$1.4</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x2" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="5" id="led456620F2024431714778525233">$0.02</a> per common share for the second quarter of <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="456618" data-tblv="5" id="led456618F2024431714778536806">2023</a>.&nbsp;&nbsp; On a year-to-date basis, the Company reported a net loss for the first six months of 2024 of $1.0 million, or $0.01 per common share, compared to net income of $14.5 million, or $.17 per common share for the first six months of 2023.&nbsp; The 2023 net income was the result of a $25 million patent license and settlement agreement entered into in February 2023, net of contingent fees and expenses.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company used $1.4 million in cash for operations for the first half of 2024, ending the quarter with $1.0 million in cash and cash equivalents.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About ParkerVision</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision, Inc. invents, develops and licenses cutting-edge, proprietary radio-frequency (RF) technologies that enable wireless solution providers to make and sell advanced wireless communication products. &nbsp;ParkerVision is engaged in a number of patent enforcement actions in the U.S. to protect patented rights that it believes are broadly infringed by others. For more information, please visit www.parkervision.com.<i> (PRKR-I)</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>
